The hotel seems to be located in Hangzhou New District, but the transportation is very convenient. It takes four stops from the hotel to reach the West Lake Scenic Area on Metro Line 1 (it takes about ten minutes to walk from the hotel to the Metro Station on Line 1). Hangzhou's bus and subway connections are very good, so don't worry about being far from West Lake and inconvenient to travel. The breakfast dishes are rich and taste good. It takes only half an hour to take a taxi from the airport to Xiaoshan Airport. Friends who have the habit of road running every day can choose here. It's really cool to run by the Qiantang River! So I said, "Master, why don't you cover the guests with your umbrella?" Then, he walked away!

I ordered Baxi ice cream cake to be delivered to the hotel, so I called the hotel front desk and asked for help collecting the cake and putting it in the refrigerator. When I got back to the hotel, they said they would give me a room directly. However, there is a catch. The hotel is newly renovated and the smell is so strong that I feel dizzy after entering. The free upgrade is just a trick of the hotel. The upgraded room may have better ventilation. Before and after check-in, the sales staff will make phone calls to upgrade the room and give good reviews. Do not believe it. There are also good reviews on the Internet. I suspect they are all fake. There is really no way for normal people to give good reviews.
Third, the service is very low-end. Express delivery and takeout are not allowed upstairs, but the waiters don't help with delivery. Isn't robot delivery a common practice?
Fourth, the catering is very poor, there are few choices, the ingredients are all carbohydrates, and the fruits feel like they have been stored for a long time.
Fifth, configuration. The bedroom and bathroom are separated, and the bedroom is closed. As a result, the whole decoration smells too great. It has not emitted poisonous gas for two or three years, and it is really not possible to move in. The air-conditioning windshield is made of inferior products, and it is rattling all night long until dawn. It kept ringing.
